 Former Chief Minister Raje said that Rajasthan is his family, leaving nowhere to go
 unhone kaha ki bijepi ke rashtriya upaadhyaksh pad kaa nishtha purvak daayitv nibhaaengi par rajasthan nahin chodengi
 Vasundhara said, 'I have already said that my doli had come to Rajasthan, now the economist will leave from here
 meraa puraa jivan mere is rajasthan parivaar ke liye samarpit rahegaa
 i am never going to back down from serving Rajasthan
 ' purv mukhyamantri jhalarapatan main bijepi kaaryakartaaon ko sambodhit kar rahi thim
 It is worth noting that the central leadership has not kept Vasundhara Raje away from the state politics, and has been trying to create a new leadership
 vasundhara ne aarope lagaaya ki 'congress jhooth bol kar satta main ai he
 He promised not to forgive the entire debt of entire farmers in 10 days, even after 40 days
 inke ghoshnaa patr main bhi yahi he par sarkaar banate hi iff and bat lag gaya
 Now talking about defaulters, short time loans and KCC
 'vasundhara ne kaha ki 'ab kisaanon kii karj maafee ke liye siem ne pradhanmantri ko patr likhaa he
 You did not write in the Congress manifesto that if you form a government, you will write a letter to the PM to forgive the debt of farmers
 ye vaada khilaafi he
 Vasundhara responded to the allegations of the Congress in which the Congress is accusing them that they promised loan waiver but did not arrange the money
 raaje ne bijepi kaaryakartaaon se kaha ki '27 lakh kisaanon kaa 50 hajaar rupye tak kaa karj byaaj or jurmaana sahit maaf kiya he
 Despite this, the CM is saying that our government gave only 2000 crores of farmers' loans whereas the truth is that apart from giving 2000 crores from our government, 5,000 crores were sanctioned from NCDC and arranging 5,000 crores from cooperative banks
 Arrangement of about 12,000 crores was made to forgive the debts of the farmers
 hamane hamaari ghoshnaa ke daayre main aane vaale tispi kshetra sahit sab kisaanon ko karj maafee kaa laabh diya
 Due to this, 60 thousand bigha land of farmers of TSP area became free of slaughter
 'abhi haal ke vidhansabha chunaav main bijepi haar gai thi
 After the defeat, Vasundhara hoped that the Congress would carry forward the policies implemented by his government in the last five years
 unhone kaha ki unki party vidhansabha main vipaksh main baithegi or janata se jude mudde uthaati rahegi
 Significantly, this time the Congress has won well in Rajasthan and has defeated the BJP a lot
 pakistani sena ne shuukravaar ko jammu kashmir ke rajouri jile main niyantran rekha par sangharsh viraam kaa ulanghan kiya

 ek jansampark adhikari (raksha) ne bataaya ki shuukravaar raat kareeb nau baje pakistan ne naushera sector main niyantran rekha par chote hathiyaaron se golibari kar bina uksaave ke sangharsh viraam ulanghan kiya or uske baad mortar daage

 tendulkar ke daure kii abhi taarikh tay nahin hui he

 The best time to cultivate saffron is during august-september
 jiske baad oktober se disambar tak kesar ke phool nikal aate hai
 Saffron is sold in millions of rupees in India
 baavjood iske kai baar moti rakam chukaane ke baad bhi log asli kesar pahchaanane main dhokhaa kha jate hai
 In this case, let us know those 5 tips, with the help of which you will be able to identify the real saffron
 pani main rang-shuddh kesar kaa rang pani main dhire-dhire dikhaai detaa he jabaki milavati kesar pani main daalane ke turant baad hi apana laal rang chhod detaa he
 Taste - Although the smell of saffron may sound sweet, but it is bitter in taste
 asli kesar kii pahchaan karne ke liye thodaa sa kesar apni jeebh par rakhkar dekhen
 If after 15-20 minutes you start feeling heat in your head, then saffron is real
 milavati kesar kaa swaad meetha hota he or ise chakhne ke baad yah aapke jeebh par laal rang chhodti he
 Identify by mixing in baking powder - adding a little baking soda in water can identify the real and fake fake saffron
 iske liye aap ek cap pani main thodaa sa baking soda len or achche se mila len
 Now note that if saffron leaves orange color during this time it is fake because when putting real saffron in water gives it dark yellow color
 nakli kesar pani main laal rang detaa he
 Try to keep it in a warm place - the threads of the saffron are always dry, break from holding, and keeping the saffron in the warm place spoils it while the fake saffron remains the same
 garm pani-kesar halke garm pani main puri tarah se ghul jaataa he
 If the fiber is not immersed in water even after keeping it in water for a long time, then saffron should be considered fake
